#<ThaCampin'Dutchpack>

    #<Description>

        By Aaron0000

        Replaces a large number of items in the game with ports and interpretations of ThaCampin'Dutchman's arsenal from Borderlands 1.

        Notes;

        Some items have options available to them, such as which item it replaces, or an alternate skin and such.

        One of the items in this mod (Thermogenesis) uses a hotfix. Be sure to merge this mod with your main patch file.

    #</Description>

    #<Individual Item Descriptions>

        #<Weapons>

            #<Bandit Weapons>

                #<Dolos>

                    Significantly increased pellet count, almost non-existent bullet speed. Increased critical hit damage.

                    Replaces Boganella by default, but can also replace Sledge's Shotgun instead.

                #</Dolos>

                #<Equuleus>

                Functions like a Revolver from Borderlands 1. Consumes three ammo per shot, increased magazine size.

                Replaces Zim.

                Note; Allows the Zim to spawn in elements other than corrosive. Non-cryo Zims will be deleted if the mod isn't run.

                #</Equuleus>

                #<Hawk>

                    No recoil. Increased accuracy.

                    Replaces Sledge's Shotgun by default, but can also replace the Boganella instead.

                #</Hawk>

                #<Traitor>

                    x4 projectile count, very high fire reate, reduced accuracy, massize magazine size. Shooting once will attempt to empty the entire magazine of ammo.

                    Replaces Meat Grinder.

                #</Traitor>

                #<Vulcan Fury>

                    Incredible fire rate and magazine size. Minimal accuracy, slow projectile speed.

                    Replaces Fusillade.

                #</Vulcan Fury>

                #<Zodiac>

                    x12 projectile count, reduced damage per projectile. Massive magazine size. Consumes two ammo per shot.

                    Replaces Badaboom.

                #</Zodiac>

            #</Bandit Weapons>

            #<Dahl Weapons>

                #<Altair>

                    x3 projectiles, reduced damage per projectile.

                    Replaces Wet Week.

                #</Altair>

                #<Barracuda>

                    Dual element - Shock Bullet, Explosive splash. Rounds twist in flight, as well as ricochet off surfaces. Increased fire rate. Shock only.

                    Replaces Major Tom.

                #</Barracuda>

                #<Komodo>

                    Four-round burst-fire outside of scopes. Divides into multiple rounds on impact that ricochet multiple times. Increased elemental damage and chance. Corrosive only.

                    Replaces Blowfly.

                #</Komodo>

            #</Dahl Weapons>

            #<Hyperion Weapons>

                #<Agonizer>

                    Explodes on contact with an enemy, penetrates enemies.

                    Replaces Logan's gun.

                #</Agonizer>

                #<Hitman>

                    Impeccable accuracy, high damage, low fire rate.

                    Replaces Fremington's Edge by default, or Invader.

                #</Hitman>

                #<Wildfire>

                    Incendiary only. Increased elemental effects. Has a unique firing pattern.

                    Replaces Heartbreaker.

                    Note; Enables Heartbreaker to spawn with sights. Sighted Heartbreakers will be deleted if you don't run the mod.

                #</Wildfire>

                #<Vanquish>

                    x2 projectiles. Reduced damage per projectile. Increased critical hit damage

                    Replaces Fatale.

                    Note; Enables Fatale to spawn with all elements. Non-Cryo Fatales will be deleted if this mod is not run.

                #</Vanquish>

                #<Black Death>

                    Creates a veritable hell of bullets upon ricohetting off a surface.

                    Replaces Viral Marketer.

                    Note; In order to launch the child projectiles, I had to take the firing mode of the Hammer Buster II (and made the barrel use a normal firing mode). Any mod that uses that firing mode is going to conflict.

                #</Black Death>

                #<Fusillation>

                    Consumes 6 ammo per shot. Increased critical hit damage, reduced fire rate. Fires a large swath of projectiles.

                    Replaces Black Snake.

                    Note; Enables the Black Snake to spawn in all elements. Non-Corrosive Black Snakes will be deleted if the mod is not run.

                #</Fusillation>

                #<Oneshot>

                    Extremely high damage, critical hit damage, and accuracy. Extrememly low fire rate and reload speed. Magazine size of 1. Consumes 5 ammo per shot. Only spawns with Hyperion parts.

                    Replaces Invader by default, but can also replace Fremington's Edge instead.

                #</Oneshot>

            #</Hyperion Weapons>

            #<Jakobs Weapons>

                #<Cricket>

                    High knockback.

                    Replaces Smasher by default, but can also replace the Maggieinstead.

                #</Cricket>

                #<Headbanger>

                    x2 projectiles.

                    Replaces Skullmasher.

                #</Headbanger>

                #<Sawed-Off>

                    High projectile count, increased damage. Minimal accuracy, magazine size of 2. Consumes 2 ammo per shot. Projectiles had a very short life span.

                    Replaces Striker.

                #</Sawed-Off>

                #<Triple>

                    Burst-fires three shots in rapid succession.

                    Replaces Maggie by default, but can also replace the Smasher instead.

                #</Triple>

                #<Railgun>

                    High damage and critical hit damage. Fires E-Tech projectiles. Consumes 2 ammo per shot.

                    Replaces Razorback.

                    Note; Forces the Razorback to spawn with a scope. Scoped Razorbacks will be deleted if this mod is not run.

                #</Railgun>

            #</Jakobs Weapons>

            #<Maliwan Weapons>

                #<Earthquake>

                    Explosive only. Ricochets upon hitting a surface.

                    Replaces Chere-Amie.

                    Note; Forces the Chere-Amie to spawn without an elemental part. Will remain as such even if the mod is not run. Does not affect existing Chere-Amies.

                #</Earthquake>

                #<Immolator>

                    Consumes 2 ammo per shot, boosted elemental damage and chance. Incendiary only.

                    Replaces Hard Reboot.

                #</Immolator>

                #<Blue Falcon>

                    Produces a large Nova upon striking a surface. Increased damage and melee damage, reduced fire rate.

                    Replaces Magma.

                #</Blue Falcon>

                #<Salvation>

                    Heals allies when shooting them. Produces transfusion orbs upon shooting enemies. Passively restores health and ammunition. Actual damage to enemies is splash only.

                    Replaces Probe.

                #</Salvation>

                #<Thermogenesis>

                    Consumes 5 ammo per shot. Fires a powerful, slow-moving laser that erupts 8 times upon striking a surface. Slow fire rate, massively increased burn damage and chance.

                    Replaces Cryophobia.

                    Note; This weapon uses the Logan's Gun projectile to achieve the erupting effect. Either use a Logan's Gun weapon replacer when using this weapon, or avoid using the Logan's Gun.

                #</Thermogenesis>

            #</Maliwan Weapons>

            #<Tediore Weapons>

                #<Garrison>

                    x4 projectiles, low accuracy.

                    Replaces Shooterang.

                #</Garrison>

                #<Apollo>

                    Fires in the shape of a triangle pointing in one of four directions.

                    Replaces Octo.

                #</Apollo>

            #</Tediore Weapons>

            #<Torgue Weapons>

                #<Abaddon>

                    Dual element - Corrosive projectile, explosive splash.

                    Replaces KerBoom.

                #</Abaddon>

                #<Cruncher>

                    Dual element - Incendiary projectile, explosive splash. Consumes four ammo per shot. Minimal accuracy, increased fire rate.

                    Replaces Moonscaper by default, but can also replace the Flakker instead.

                #</Cruncher>

                #<Lacerta>

                    Consumes four ammo per shot. Fires a slow moving projectile that divides and multiple projectiles after a short period of time.

                    Replaces KerBoom.

                #</Lacerta>

                #<Painbringer>

                    Functions like a revolver from Borderlands 1. Consumes 3 ammo per shot. Dual element - Shock projectile, explosive splash. Increased reload speed. Large explosion radius.

                    Replaces 88 Fragnum.

                    Note; Has an option for an alternative skin.

                #</Painbringer>

            #</Torgue Weapons>

            #<Vladof Weapons>

                #<Guerilla>

                    Significantly increased fire rate, increased weapon stability.

                    Replaces The Machine.

                #</Guerilla>

                #<Laelaps>

                    Increases movement speed when held.

                    Replaces Proletarian Revolution.

                #</Laelaps>

                #<Spitfire>

                    Consumes 3 ammo per shot. x8 projectiles. Reduced damage per projectile, minimal accuracy.

                    Replaces Shredifier.

                #</Spitfire>

            #</Vladof Weapons>

        #</Weapons>

        #<Shields>

            #<Flatline>

                Has a capacity of 1, no ability to recharge passively. Lowers fight For your Life Time down to the minimum. Produces a powerful nuclear explosion upon going into Fight for your Life.

                Replaces Deadly Bloom.

                Note; Enables Deadly Bloom to spawn with non-explosive elemental resistance capacitors. Deadly Blooms with elemental resistance parts will be deleted if the mod is not run.

            #</Flatline>

            #<Godspeed>

                Minimal shield capacity. Dramatically increases movement speed. Chance to reflect bullets.

                Replaces Kala.

            #</Godspeed>

            #<Primrose>

                Low capacity, regenerates 12.5% of your health every second. Increases Action Skill cooldown rate.

                Replaces Neogenator.

            #</Primrose>

            #<Undying>

                High capacity, no health penalty. Significantly extends Fight for your Life time.

                Replaces Fabled Tortoise.

            #</Undying>

        #</Shields>

    #</Individual Item Descriptions>

    #<Weapons>

        #<Bandit>

            #<Legendary>

                #<Dolos><MUT>

                    #<Boganella replacer (Default)>

                        #<Name/Red Text>

                            set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Title__Unique_Boganella PartName Dolos

                            set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Name.Title__Unique_Boganella:AttributePresentationDefinition_8 NoConstraintText You just activated my trap card!

                        #</Name/Red Text>

                        #<Rarity>

                            set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Barrel.SG_Barrel_Bandit_Boganella rarity (basevalueattribute=none)

                            set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Barrel.SG_Barrel_Bandit_Boganella rarity (BaseValueConstant=5)

                        #</Rarity>

                        #<Stats>

                            set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Barrel.SG_Barrel_Bandit_Boganella AttributeSlotUpgrades ((SlotName="WeaponSpread",GradeIncrease=-34,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="AccuracyMin",GradeIncrease=-4,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponDamage",GradeIncrease=7,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponAccuracyImpulse",GradeIncrease=-14,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponFireRate",GradeIncrease=-12,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponMagSize",GradeIncrease=2,bActivateSlot=True))

                            #set GD_Cork_Weap_Shotgun.Barrel.SG_Barrel_Bandit_Boganella BehaviorProviderDefinition None

                        #</Stats>
